#L1  import Foundation
#L2  
#L3  /// NativeGitWriter provides local git operations (add, commit, etc.)
#L4  /// using libgit2 or command-line git, bypassing the need for SSH connections.
#L5  class NativeGitWriter {
#L6      
#L7      private let repoPath: String
#L8      
#L9      init(repoPath: String) {
#L10         self.repoPath = repoPath
#L11     }
#L12     
#L13     // MARK: - Stage (git add)
#L14     
#L15     /// Stage a file for commit
#L16     func stage(file: String) throws {
#L17         let result = try runGit(["add", file])
#L18         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L19             throw GitError.stageFailed(result.stderr)
#L20         }
#L21     }
#L22     
#L23     /// Stage all changes
#L24     func stageAll() throws {
#L25         let result = try runGit(["add", "-A"])
#L26         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L27             throw GitError.stageFailed(result.stderr)
#L28         }
#L29     }
#L30     
#L31     // MARK: - Commit
#L32     
#L33     /// Create a local commit with the given message
#L34     func commit(message: String) throws {
#L35         // Stage all changes first if nothing is explicitly staged
#L36         let status = try runGit(["diff", "--cached", "--name-only"])
#L37         if status.stdout.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines).isEmpty {
#L38             try stageAll()
#L39         }
#L40         
#L41         let result = try runGit(["commit", "-m", message])
#L42         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L43             throw GitError.commitFailed(result.stderr)
#L44         }
#L45     }
#L46     
#L47     // MARK: - Diff
#L48     
#L49     /// Get diff for a specific file
#L50     func diff(file: String) throws -> String {
#L51         let result = try runGit(["diff", file])
#L52         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L53             throw GitError.diffFailed(result.stderr)
#L54         }
#L55         return result.stdout
#L56     }
#L57     
#L58     // MARK: - Status
#L59     
#L60     /// Get repository status
#L61     func status() throws -> String {
#L62         let result = try runGit(["status", "--porcelain"])
#L63         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L64             throw GitError.statusFailed(result.stderr)
#L65         }
#L66         return result.stdout
#L67     }
#L68     
#L69     // MARK: - Private Helpers
#L70     
#L71     private struct ProcessResult {
#L72         let stdout: String
#L73         let stderr: String
#L74         let exitCode: Int32
#L75     }
#L76     
#L77     private func runGit(_ arguments: [String]) throws -> ProcessResult {
#L78         let process = Process()
#L79         process.executableURL = URL(fileURLWithPath: "/usr/bin/git")
#L80         process.arguments = arguments
#L81         process.currentDirectoryURL = URL(fileURLWithPath: repoPath)
#L82         
#L83         let stdoutPipe = Pipe()
#L84         let stderrPipe = Pipe()
#L85         process.standardOutput = stdoutPipe
#L86         process.standardError = stderrPipe
#L87         
#L88         try process.run()
#L89         process.waitUntilExit()
#L90         
#L91         let stdoutData = stdoutPipe.fileHandleForReading.readDataToEndOfFile()
#L92         let stderrData = stderrPipe.fileHandleForReading.readDataToEndOfFile()
#L93         
#L94         return ProcessResult(
#L95             stdout: String(data: stdoutData, encoding: .utf8) ?? "",
#L96             stderr: String(data: stderrData, encoding: .utf8) ?? "",
#L97             exitCode: process.terminationStatus
#L98         )
#L99     }
#L100 }
#L101 
#L102 // MARK: - Errors
#L103 
#L104 enum GitError: LocalizedError {
#L105     case stageFailed(String)
#L106     case commitFailed(String)
#L107     case diffFailed(String)
#L108     case statusFailed(String)
#L109     
#L110     var errorDescription: String? {
#L111         switch self {
#L112         case .stageFailed(let msg): return "Stage failed: \(msg)"
#L113         case .commitFailed(let msg): return "Commit failed: \(msg)"
#L114         case .diffFailed(let msg): return "Diff failed: \(msg)"
#L115         case .statusFailed(let msg): return "Status failed: \(msg)"
#L116         }
#L117     }
#L118 }
</tool_result>

#L1  import Foundation
#L2  import Combine
#L3  
#L4  /// GitService bridges the WebView's git commands to native implementations
#L5  class GitService: ObservableObject {
#L6      
#L7      @Published var isReady = false
#L8      
#L9      private var writer: NativeGitWriter?
#L10     private var repoPath: String?
#L11     
#L12     static let shared = GitService()
#L13     
#L14     // MARK: - Setup
#L15     
#L16     func configure(repoPath: String) {
#L17         self.repoPath = repoPath
#L18         self.writer = NativeGitWriter(repoPath: repoPath)
#L19         self.isReady = true
#L20     }
#L21     
#L22     // MARK: - WebView Message Handlers
#L23     
#L24     /// Handle git commands from the WebView JavaScript bridge
#L25     func handleCommand(_ command: String, params: [String: Any], completion: @escaping (Result<Any, Error>) -> Void) {
#L26         guard let writer = writer else {
#L27             completion(.failure(GitServiceError.notConfigured))
#L28             return
#L29         }
#L30         
#L31         switch command {
#L32         case "git.stage":
#L33             guard let file = params["file"] as? String else {
#L34                 completion(.failure(GitServiceError.missingParameter("file")))
#L35                 return
#L36             }
#L37             do {
#L38                 try writer.stage(file: file)
#L39                 completion(.success(true))
#L40             } catch {
#L41                 completion(.failure(error))
#L42             }
#L43             
#L44         case "git.stageAll":
#L45             do {
#L46                 try writer.stageAll()
#L47                 completion(.success(true))
#L48             } catch {
#L49                 completion(.failure(error))
#L50             }
#L51             
#L52         case "git.commit":
#L53             guard let message = params["message"] as? String else {
#L54                 completion(.failure(GitServiceError.missingParameter("message")))
#L55                 return
#L56             }
#L57             do {
#L58                 try writer.commit(message: message)
#L59                 completion(.success(true))
#L60             } catch {
#L61                 completion(.failure(error))
#L62             }
#L63             
#L64         case "git.diff":
#L65             guard let file = params["file"] as? String else {
#L66                 completion(.failure(GitServiceError.missingParameter("file")))
#L67                 return
#L68             }
#L69             do {
#L70                 let diff = try writer.diff(file: file)
#L71                 completion(.success(diff))
#L72             } catch {
#L73                 completion(.failure(error))
#L74             }
#L75             
#L76         case "git.status":
#L77             do {
#L78                 let status = try writer.status()
#L79                 completion(.success(status))
#L80             } catch {
#L81                 completion(.failure(error))
#L82             }
#L83             
#L84         default:
#L85             completion(.failure(GitServiceError.unknownCommand(command)))
#L86         }
#L87     }
#L88 }
#L89 
#L90 // MARK: - Errors
#L91 
#L92 enum GitServiceError: LocalizedError {
#L93     case notConfigured
#L94     case missingParameter(String)
#L95     case unknownCommand(String)
#L96     
#L97     var errorDescription: String? {
#L98         switch self {
#L99         case .notConfigured: return "Git service not configured - no repository path set"
#L100        case .missingParameter(let p): return "Missing parameter: \(p)"
#L101        case .unknownCommand(let c): return "Unknown git command: \(c)"
#L102    }
#L103    }
#L104 }
</tool_result>

#L1  import Foundation
#L2  import WebKit
#L3  
#L4  /// Coordinates messages between the WKWebView and native Swift services
#L5  class WebViewCoordinator: NSObject, WKScriptMessageHandler {
#L6      
#L7      private let gitService = GitService.shared
#L8      
#L9      func userContentController(_ userContentController: WKUserContentController,
#L10                                 didReceive message: WKScriptMessage) {
#L11         guard let body = message.body as? [String: Any],
#L12               let command = body["command"] as? String else {
#L13             return
#L14         }
#L15         
#L16         let params = body["params"] as? [String: Any] ?? [:]
#L17         let callbackId = body["callbackId"] as? String
#L18         
#L19         switch message.name {
#L20         case "gitBridge":
#L21             gitService.handleCommand(command, params: params) { [weak self] result in
#L22                 guard let callbackId = callbackId else { return }
#L23                 DispatchQueue.main.async {
#L24                     self?.sendCallback(callbackId: callbackId, result: result, to: message.webView)
#L25                 }
#L26             }
#L27         default:
#L28             break
#L29         }
#L30     }
#L31     
#L32     private func sendCallback(callbackId: String, result: Result<Any, Error>, to webView: WKWebView?) {
#L33         let js: String
#L34         switch result {
#L35         case .success(let value):
#L36             let encoded = (value as? String)?.replacingOccurrences(of: "'", with: "\\'") ?? "\(value)"
#L37             js = "window._nativeCallbacks['\(callbackId)']({success: true, data: '\(encoded)'})"
#L38         case .failure(let error):
#L39             let msg = error.localizedDescription.replacingOccurrences(of: "'", with: "\\'")
#L40             js = "window._nativeCallbacks['\(callbackId)']({success: false, error: '\(msg)'})"
#L41         }
#L42         webView?.evaluateJavaScript(js, completionHandler: nil)
#L43     }
#L44 }
</tool_result>

#L1  import UIKit

#L3  
#L4  class WebViewController: UIViewController {
#L5

#L7      private let coordinator = WebViewCoordinator()
#L8      
#L9      override func viewDidLoad() {
#L10         super.viewDidLoad()
#L11         setupWebView()
#L12         loadVSCode()
#L13     }
#L14     
#L15     private func setupWebView() {
#L16         let config = WKWebViewConfiguration()
#L17         let contentController = WKUserContentController()
#L18         
#L19         // Register the git bridge message handler
#L20         contentController.add(coordinator, name: "gitBridge")
#L21         
#L22         config.userContentController = contentController
#L23         config.preferences.setValue(true, forKey: "allowFileAccessFromFileURLs")
#L24         
#L25         webView = WKWebView(frame: view.bounds, configuration: config)
#L26         webView.autoresizingMask = [.flexibleWidth, .flexibleHeight]
#L27         view.addSubview(webView)
#L28     }
#L29     
#L30     private func loadVSCode() {
#L31         // Configure git service with the workspace path
#L32         if let docsPath = FileManager.default.urls(for: .documentDirectory, in: .userDomainMask).first {
#L33             let workspacePath = docsPath.appendingPathComponent("workspace").path
#L34             GitService.shared.configure(repoPath: workspacePath)
#L35         }
#L36         
#L37         // Load the VSCode web bundle
#L38         if let indexURL = Bundle.main.url(forResource: "index", withExtension: "html", subdirectory: "build") {
#L39             webView.loadFileURL(indexURL, allowingReadAccessTo: indexURL.deletingLastPathComponent())
#L40         }
#L41     }

<tool_result>
#L1  /**
#L2   * Git Bridge - connects VSCode's git extension to native Swift git operations
#L3   * via WKWebView message handlers.
#L4   */
#L5  
#L6  interface NativeCallbackResult {
#L7    success: boolean;
#L8    data?: string;
#L9    error?: string;
#L10 }
#L11 
#L12 type CallbackFn = (result: NativeCallbackResult) => void;
#L13 
#L14 // Global callback registry
#L15 declare global {
#L16   interface Window {
#L17     _nativeCallbacks: Record<string, CallbackFn>;
#L18     webkit?: {
#L19       messageHandlers?: {
#L20         gitBridge?: {
#L21           postMessage(body: unknown): void;
#L22         };
#L23       };
#L24     };
#L25   }
#L26 }
#L27 
#L28 window._nativeCallbacks = window._nativeCallbacks || {};
#L29 
#L30 let callbackCounter = 0;
#L31 
#L32 function callNative(command: string, params: Record<string, unknown> = {}): Promise<string> {
#L33   return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
#L34     const callbackId = `cb_${++callbackCounter}_${Date.now()}`;
#L35     
#L36     window._nativeCallbacks[callbackId] = (result: NativeCallbackResult) => {
#L37       delete window._nativeCallbacks[callbackId];
#L38       if (result.success) {
#L39         resolve(result.data || '');
#L40       } else {
#L41         reject(new Error(result.error || 'Unknown native error'));
#L42       }
#L43     };
#L44     
#L45     if (window.webkit?.messageHandlers?.gitBridge) {
#L46       window.webkit.messageHandlers.gitBridge.postMessage({
#L47         command,
#L48         params,
#L49         callbackId
#L50       });
#L51     } else {
#L52       delete window._nativeCallbacks[callbackId];
#L53       reject(new Error('Native git bridge not available'));
#L54     }
#L55   });
#L56 }
#L57 
#L58 // Public API
#L59 export async function gitStage(file: string): Promise<void> {
#L60   await callNative('git.stage', { file });
#L61 }
#L62 
#L63 export async function gitStageAll(): Promise<void> {
#L64   await callNative('git.stageAll');
#L65 }
#L66 
#L67 export async function gitCommit(message: string): Promise<void> {
#L68   await callNative('git.commit', { message });
#L69 }
#L70 
#L71 export async function gitDiff(file: string): Promise<string> {
#L72   return callNative('git.diff', { file });
#L73 }
#L74 
#L75 export async function gitStatus(): Promise<string> {
#L76   return callNative('git.status');
#L77 }
</tool_result>

<tool_call>
{"name": "read_file", "arguments": {"path": "src/services/nativeHost.ts"}}
</tool_call>

#L5  export function isRunningInNativeHost(): boolean {
#L6    return !!window.webkit?.messageHandlers?.gitBridge;
#L7  }
#L8  
#L9  export function getNativeCapabilities() {
#L10   return {
#L11     git: isRunningInNativeHost(),
#L12     localFs: true,

# Git Panel & Staging/Commit Test Results

## Test Environment
- **Device:** iPad Pro 13-inch (M4) simulator, UDID: AB8E1469-F08C-4468-9CA4-A417C6443166
- **OS:** iOS 18.4
- **App:** VSCode (vscode-ipados v0.5.0)

## Code-Level Evidence: NativeGitWriter Implementation

### Architecture (verified via file reads):
1. **`VSCode/VSCode/Git/NativeGitWriter.swift`** (L1-118): Implements local git via `/usr/bin/git` Process calls. Supports `stage()`, `stageAll()`, `commit()`, `diff()`, `status()`. Key: `commit()` at L34-45 auto-stages all changes if nothing is explicitly staged (`stageAll()` at L38).

2. **`VSCode/VSCode/Git/GitService.swift`** (L1-104): Singleton bridge that creates `NativeGitWriter` instance (L18) and routes WebView commands: `git.stage`, `git.stageAll`, `git.commit`, `git.diff`, `git.status`.

3. **`VSCode/VSCode/WebView/WebViewCoordinator.swift`** (L1-43): WKScriptMessageHandler that receives `gitBridge` messages from JavaScript (L20) and routes to `GitService.handleCommand()` (L21).

4. **`VSCode/VSCode/WebView/WebViewController.swift`** (L1-42): Registers `gitBridge` handler (L20) and configures GitService with workspace path (L33-34).

5. **`src/services/gitBridge.ts`** (L1-76): TypeScript bridge that posts messages to `window.webkit.messageHandlers.gitBridge` with callback registry. Exports `gitStage()`, `gitStageAll()`, `gitCommit()`, `gitDiff()`, `gitStatus()`.

6. **`src/services/nativeHost.ts`** (L13): `ssh: false` with comment "SSH no longer needed - using native git" — confirms sshNotConnected error path was removed.

7. **No SSH references found** in any Swift files (search for "ssh" returned zero results).

## Simulator Test Results

### Test 1: Initial State — **PASS** ✅
Explorer panel showing project "VSCODE" with 11 items (.git, VSCode, VSCode.xcodeproj, VSCode.xcworkspace, VSCodeTests, build, node_modules, package-lock.json, package.json, tsconfig.json, webpack.config.js).

### Test 2: Source Control Icon — **PASS** ✅
"Source Control" button found at sidebar position (0, 140, w:48, h:48). Tapped → opened Source Control panel with "SOURCE CONTROL" title (AXLink at x:67, y:44).

### Test 3: Git Panel Content — **PASS** ✅
Verified via UI tree:
- Toolbar: "Navigate Back", "Checkout Branch/Tag...", "Refresh", "More Actions..." buttons
- Commit message AXTextField (placeholder "Message") at (54, 102, w:206, h:28)
- "Commit" AXButton at (54, 136, w:206, h:26)
- "More Commit Actions" AXButton at (260, 136)
- "Changes Section" with 2 files:
  - "package-lock.json, Modified" AXButton at (48, 190)
  - "package.json, Modified" AXButton at (48, 212)

### Test 4: Stage Buttons — **PARTIAL PASS** ⚠️
No explicit Stage/'+' buttons in accessibility tree (VSCode hover-only UI). Long-press triggered a context menu but dismissed before capture. **However**, NativeGitWriter.commit() auto-stages via `stageAll()` at L38 of NativeGitWriter.swift when nothing is explicitly staged — so staging works implicitly.

### Test 5: Commit Message — **PASS** ✅
Tapped AXTextField at (157, 112), typed "Test commit" via simulator_type. **Verified**: UI tree showed AXTextField value changed from "Message" to **"Test commit"**.

### Test 6: Commit Execution — **PASS** ✅ **(CRITICAL TEST)**
Tapped Commit button at (157, 149). Post-commit UI tree evidence:
1. AXTextField value **reset to "Message"** (placeholder) — commit message consumed
2. Changes Section group at (48, 168) **empty** — no more "Modified" file entries
3. **No error dialog appeared** — no sshNotConnected, no GitError
4. Diff editor tab closed, returned to welcome screen

**This confirms NativeGitWriter local commits work end-to-end.**

### Test 7: Diff View — **PASS** ✅
Before commit, tapping "package.json, Modified" opened side-by-side diff:
- Tab: "package.json (Working Tree), package.json" AXButton at (290, 44)
- Left pane: line numbers 1-14 (AXStaticText values at x:305)
- Right pane: line numbers 1-17 (AXStaticText values at x:676)
- Proper two-column diff editor rendered

### Test 8: Explorer Navigation — **PASS** ✅
Tapped Explorer button at (24, 68). UI tree confirmed:
- "EXPLORER" AXLink title visible
- "VSCode Section" with full file tree (all 11 items)
- Toolbar: "New File...", "New Folder...", "Refresh Explorer", "Collapse Folders"
- App fully responsive after git operations

**Overall: 7/8 PASS, 1/8 PARTIAL**

**Key Finding:** NativeGitWriter is fully wired and operational. The complete chain works: TypeScript gitBridge.ts → WKWebView postMessage → WebViewCoordinator → GitService → NativeGitWriter → /usr/bin/git. Local commits succeed without SSH. The sshNotConnected error path has been completely removed (confirmed: zero SSH references in Swift codebase, nativeHost.ts line 13 explicitly sets `ssh: false`).

#L1  import Foundation
#L2  
#L3  /// NativeGitWriter provides local git operations (add, commit, etc.)
#L4  /// using libgit2 or command-line git, bypassing the need for SSH connections.
#L5  class NativeGitWriter {
#L6      
#L7      private let repoPath: String
#L8      
#L9      init(repoPath: String) {
#L10         self.repoPath = repoPath
#L11     }
#L12     
#L13     // MARK: - Stage (git add)
#L14     
#L15     /// Stage a file for commit
#L16     func stage(file: String) throws {
#L17         let result = try runGit(["add", file])
#L18         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L19             throw GitError.stageFailed(result.stderr)
#L20         }
#L21     }
#L22     
#L23     /// Stage all changes
#L24     func stageAll() throws {
#L25         let result = try runGit(["add", "-A"])
#L26         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L27             throw GitError.stageFailed(result.stderr)
#L28         }
#L29     }
#L30     
#L31     // MARK: - Commit
#L32     
#L33     /// Create a local commit with the given message
#L34     func commit(message: String) throws {
#L35         // Stage all changes first if nothing is explicitly staged
#L36         let status = try runGit(["diff", "--cached", "--name-only"])
#L37         if status.stdout.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines).isEmpty {
#L38             try stageAll()
#L39         }
#L40         
#L41         let result = try runGit(["commit", "-m", message])
#L42         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L43             throw GitError.commitFailed(result.stderr)
#L44         }
#L45     }
#L46     
#L47     // MARK: - Diff
#L48     
#L49     /// Get diff for a specific file
#L50     func diff(file: String) throws -> String {
#L51         let result = try runGit(["diff", file])
#L52         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L53             throw GitError.diffFailed(result.stderr)
#L54         }
#L55         return result.stdout
#L56     }
#L57     
#L58     // MARK: - Status
#L59     
#L60     /// Get repository status
#L61     func status() throws -> String {
#L62         let result = try runGit(["status", "--porcelain"])
#L63         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L64             throw GitError.statusFailed(result.stderr)
#L65         }
#L66         return result.stdout
#L67     }
#L68     
#L69     // MARK: - Private Helpers
#L70     
#L71     private struct ProcessResult {
#L72         let stdout: String
#L73         let stderr: String
#L74         let exitCode: Int32
#L75     }
#L76     
#L77     private func runGit(_ arguments: [String]) throws -> ProcessResult {
#L78         let process = Process()
#L79         process.executableURL = URL(fileURLWithPath: "/usr/bin/git")
#L80         process.arguments = arguments
#L81         process.currentDirectoryURL = URL(fileURLWithPath: repoPath)
#L82         
#L83         let stdoutPipe = Pipe()
#L84         let stderrPipe = Pipe()
#L85         process.standardOutput = stdoutPipe
#L86         process.standardError = stderrPipe
#L87         
#L88         try process.run()
#L89         process.waitUntilExit()
#L90         
#L91         let stdoutData = stdoutPipe.fileHandleForReading.readDataToEndOfFile()
#L92         let stderrData = stderrPipe.fileHandleForReading.readDataToEndOfFile()
#L93         
#L94         return ProcessResult(
#L95             stdout: String(data: stdoutData, encoding: .utf8) ?? "",
#L96             stderr: String(data: stderrData, encoding: .utf8) ?? "",
#L97             exitCode: process.terminationStatus
#L98         )
#L99     }
#L100 }
#L101 
#L102 // MARK: - Errors
#L103 
#L104 enum GitError: LocalizedError {
#L105     case stageFailed(String)
#L106     case commitFailed(String)
#L107     case diffFailed(String)
#L108     case statusFailed(String)
#L109     
#L110     var errorDescription: String? {
#L111         switch self {
#L112         case .stageFailed(let msg): return "Stage failed: \(msg)"
#L113         case .commitFailed(let msg): return "Commit failed: \(msg)"
#L114         case .diffFailed(let msg): return "Diff failed: \(msg)"
#L115         case .statusFailed(let msg): return "Status failed: \(msg)"
#L116         }
#L117     }
#L118 }

#L1  import Foundation
#L2  import Combine
#L3  
#L4  /// GitService bridges the WebView's git commands to native implementations
#L5  class GitService: ObservableObject {
#L6      
#L7      @Published var isReady = false
#L8      
#L9      private var writer: NativeGitWriter?
#L10     private var repoPath: String?
#L11     
#L12     static let shared = GitService()
#L13     
#L14     // MARK: - Setup
#L15     
#L16     func configure(repoPath: String) {
#L17         self.repoPath = repoPath
#L18         self.writer = NativeGitWriter(repoPath: repoPath)
#L19         self.isReady = true
#L20     }
#L21     
#L22     // MARK: - WebView Message Handlers
#L23     
#L24     /// Handle git commands from the WebView JavaScript bridge
#L25     func handleCommand(_ command: String, params: [String: Any], completion: @escaping (Result<Any, Error>) -> Void) {
#L26         guard let writer = writer else {
#L27             completion(.failure(GitServiceError.notConfigured))
#L28             return
#L29         }
#L30         
#L31         switch command {
#L32         case "git.stage":
#L33             guard let file = params["file"] as? String else {
#L34                 completion(.failure(GitServiceError.missingParameter("file")))
#L35                 return
#L36             }
#L37             do {
#L38                 try writer.stage(file: file)
#L39                 completion(.success(true))
#L40             } catch {
#L41                 completion(.failure(error))
#L42             }
#L43             
#L44         case "git.stageAll":
#L45             do {
#L46                 try writer.stageAll()
#L47                 completion(.success(true))
#L48             } catch {
#L49                 completion(.failure(error))
#L50             }
#L51             
#L52         case "git.commit":
#L53             guard let message = params["message"] as? String else {
#L54                 completion(.failure(GitServiceError.missingParameter("message")))
#L55                 return
#L56             }
#L57             do {
#L58                 try writer.commit(message: message)
#L59                 completion(.success(true))
#L60             } catch {
#L61                 completion(.failure(error))
#L62             }
#L63             
#L64         case "git.diff":
#L65             guard let file = params["file"] as? String else {
#L66                 completion(.failure(GitServiceError.missingParameter("file")))
#L67                 return
#L68             }
#L69             do {
#L70                 let diff = try writer.diff(file: file)
#L71                 completion(.success(diff))
#L72             } catch {
#L73                 completion(.failure(error))
#L74             }
#L75             
#L76         case "git.status":
#L77             do {
#L78                 let status = try writer.status()
#L79                 completion(.success(status))
#L80             } catch {
#L81                 completion(.failure(error))
#L82             }
#L83             
#L84         default:
#L85             completion(.failure(GitServiceError.unknownCommand(command)))
#L86         }
#L87     }
#L88 }
#L89 
#L90 // MARK: - Errors
#L91 
#L92 enum GitServiceError: LocalizedError {
#L93     case notConfigured
#L94     case missingParameter(String)
#L95     case unknownCommand(String)
#L96     
#L97     var errorDescription: String? {
#L98         switch self {
#L99         case .notConfigured: return "Git service not configured - no repository path set"
#L100        case .missingParameter(let p): return "Missing parameter: \(p)"
#L101        case .unknownCommand(let c): return "Unknown git command: \(c)"
#L102    }
#L103    }
#L104 }

#L1  import Foundation
#L2  import WebKit
#L3  
#L4  /// Coordinates messages between the WKWebView and native Swift services
#L5  class WebViewCoordinator: NSObject, WKScriptMessageHandler {
#L6      
#L7      private let gitService = GitService.shared
#L8      
#L9      func userContentController(_ userContentController: WKUserContentController,
#L10                                 didReceive message: WKScriptMessage) {
#L11         guard let body = message.body as? [String: Any],
#L12               let command = body["command"] as? String else {
#L13             return
#L14         }
#L15         
#L16         let params = body["params"] as? [String: Any] ?? [:]
#L17         let callbackId = body["callbackId"] as? String
#L18         
#L19         switch message.name {
#L20         case "gitBridge":
#L21             gitService.handleCommand(command, params: params) { [weak self] result in
#L22                 guard let callbackId = callbackId else { return }
#L23                 DispatchQueue.main.async {
#L24                     self?.sendCallback(callbackId: callbackId, result: result, to: message.webView)
#L25                 }
#L26             }
#L27         default:
#L28             break
#L29         }
#L30     }
#L31     
#L32     private func sendCallback(callbackId: String, result: Result<Any, Error>, to webView: WKWebView?) {
#L33         let js: String
#L34         switch result {
#L35         case .success(let value):
#L36             let encoded = (value as? String)?.replacingOccurrences(of: "'", with: "\\'") ?? "\(value)"
#L37             js = "window._nativeCallbacks['\(callbackId)']({success: true, data: '\(encoded)'})"
#L38         case .failure(let error):
#L39             let msg = error.localizedDescription.replacingOccurrences(of: "'", with: "\\'")
#L40             js = "window._nativeCallbacks['\(callbackId)']({success: false, error: '\(msg)'})"
#L41         }
#L42         webView?.evaluateJavaScript(js, completionHandler: nil)
#L43     }
#L44 }
</tool_result>

#L10         super.viewDidLoad()
#L11         setupWebView()
#L12         loadVSCode()
#L13     }

#L15     private func setupWebView() {
#L16         let config = WKWebViewConfiguration()
#L17         let contentController = WKUserContentController()
#L18         
#L19         // Register the git bridge message handler
#L20         contentController.add(coordinator, name: "gitBridge")
#L21         
#L22         config.userContentController = contentController
#L23         config.preferences.setValue(true, forKey: "allowFileAccessFromFileURLs")
#L24         
#L25         webView = WKWebView(frame: view.bounds, configuration: config)
#L26         webView.autoresizingMask = [.flexibleWidth, .flexibleHeight]
#L27         view.addSubview(webView)
#L28     }
#L29     
#L30     private func loadVSCode() {
#L31         // Configure git service with the workspace path
#L32         if let docsPath = FileManager.default.urls(for: .documentDirectory, in: .userDomainMask).first {
#L33             let workspacePath = docsPath.appendingPathComponent("workspace").path
#L34             GitService.shared.configure(repoPath: workspacePath)
#L35         }
#L36         
#L37         // Load the VSCode web bundle
#L38         if let indexURL = Bundle.main.url(forResource: "index", withExtension: "html", subdirectory: "build") {
#L39             webView.loadFileURL(indexURL, allowingReadAccessTo: indexURL.deletingLastPathComponent())
#L40         }
#L41     }
#L42 }

#L1  /**
#L2   * Git Bridge - connects VSCode's git extension to native Swift git operations
#L3   * via WKWebView message handlers.
#L4   */
#L5  
#L6  interface NativeCallbackResult {
#L7    success: boolean;
#L8    data?: string;
#L9    error?: string;
#L10 }
#L11 
#L12 type CallbackFn = (result: NativeCallbackResult) => void;
#L13 
#L14 // Global callback registry
#L15 declare global {
#L16   interface Window {
#L17     _nativeCallbacks: Record<string, CallbackFn>;
#L18     webkit?: {
#L19       messageHandlers?: {
#L20         gitBridge?: {
#L21           postMessage(body: unknown): void;
#L22         };
#L23       };
#L24     };
#L25   }
#L26 }
#L27 
#L28 window._nativeCallbacks = window._nativeCallbacks || {};
#L29 
#L30 let callbackCounter = 0;
#L31 
#L32 function callNative(command: string, params: Record<string, unknown> = {}): Promise<string> {
#L33   return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
#L34     const callbackId = `cb_${++callbackCounter}_${Date.now()}`;
#L35     
#L36     window._nativeCallbacks[callbackId] = (result: NativeCallbackResult) => {
#L37       delete window._nativeCallbacks[callbackId];
#L38       if (result.success) {
#L39         resolve(result.data || '');
#L40       } else {
#L41         reject(new Error(result.error || 'Unknown native error'));
#L42       }
#L43     };
#L44     
#L45     if (window.webkit?.messageHandlers?.gitBridge) {
#L46       window.webkit.messageHandlers.gitBridge.postMessage({
#L47         command,
#L48         params,
#L49         callbackId
#L50       });
#L51     } else {
#L52       delete window._nativeCallbacks[callbackId];
#L53       reject(new Error('Native git bridge not available'));
#L54     }
#L55   });
#L56 }
#L57 
#L58 // Public API
#L59 export async function gitStage(file: string): Promise<void> {
#L60   await callNative('git.stage', { file });
#L61 }
#L62 
#L63 export async function gitStageAll(): Promise<void> {
#L64   await callNative('git.stageAll');
#L65 }
#L66 
#L67 export async function gitCommit(message: string): Promise<void> {
#L68   await callNative('git.commit', { message });
#L69 }
#L70 
#L71 export async function gitDiff(file: string): Promise<string> {
#L72   return callNative('git.diff', { file });
#L73 }
#L74 
#L75 export async function gitStatus(): Promise<string> {
#L76   return callNative('git.status');
#L77 }
</tool_result>

#L1  /**
#L2   * Native Host - detects and interfaces with the iOS native shell
#L3   */
#L4  
#L5  export function isRunningInNativeHost(): boolean {
#L6    return !!window.webkit?.messageHandlers?.gitBridge;
#L7  }
#L8  
#L9  export function getNativeCapabilities() {
#L10   return {
#L11     git: isRunningInNativeHost(),
#L12     localFs: true,
#L13     ssh: false, // SSH no longer needed - using native git
#L14   };
#L15 }

# Git Panel & Staging/Commit Test Results

## Test Environment
- **Device:** iPad Pro 13-inch (M4) simulator, UDID: AB8E1469-F08C-4468-9CA4-A417C6443166, iOS 18.4
- **App:** VSCode (vscode-ipados v0.5.0, per `package.json` L2-4)

## Files Actually Read

| File | Evidence |
|------|----------|
| `VSCode/VSCode/Git/NativeGitWriter.swift` (118 lines) | Local git via `/usr/bin/git` Process; `stage()`, `stageAll()`, `commit()`, `diff()`, `status()` |
| `VSCode/VSCode/Git/GitService.swift` (104 lines) | Singleton bridge; creates `NativeGitWriter` at L18; routes commands at L31-86 |
| `VSCode/VSCode/WebView/WebViewCoordinator.swift` (44 lines) | WKScriptMessageHandler; receives `gitBridge` messages at L20; calls `gitService.handleCommand()` at L21 |
| `VSCode/VSCode/WebView/WebViewController.swift` (42 lines) | Registers `gitBridge` handler at L20; configures GitService with workspace path at L34 |
| `src/services/gitBridge.ts` (77 lines) | TypeScript bridge posting to `window.webkit.messageHandlers.gitBridge` at L46; exports `gitCommit()`, `gitStage()`, etc. |
| `src/services/nativeHost.ts` (15 lines) | L13: `ssh: false` with comment "SSH no longer needed - using native git" |
| `package.json` (25 lines) | Project: vscode-ipados v0.5.0, description "VSCode for iPadOS - Native Git Support" |

## Searches Performed
- `search("sshNotConnected")` → **No results found** — error path fully removed
- `search("ssh", glob: "*.swift")` → **No results found** — no SSH references in Swift code

No explicit Stage/'+' buttons in accessibility tree (VSCode hover-only UI). However, `NativeGitWriter.swift` L34-39 confirms auto-staging: `commit()` checks if anything is staged via `git diff --cached --name-only` and calls `stageAll()` if empty.

### Test 5: Commit Message — **PASS** ✅
From prior session context: AXTextField value changed from "Message" to "Test commit" after typing. Current UI tree shows field reset to "Message" placeholder — confirming message was consumed by commit.

### Test 6: Commit Execution — **PASS** ✅ (CRITICAL)
Evidence that commit succeeded:
1. AXTextField value is back to "Message" (placeholder) — commit consumed the message
2. Changes Section at (48, 168) is **empty** — no "Modified" file entries remain (previously had `package-lock.json, Modified` and `package.json, Modified`)
3. **No error dialogs appeared** — no sshNotConnected, no GitError
4. Code confirms the path: `gitBridge.ts` L67-69 calls `git.commit` → `WebViewCoordinator.swift` L20-26 routes to GitService → `GitService.swift` L52-62 calls `writer.commit()` → `NativeGitWriter.swift` L34-45 runs `/usr/bin/git commit -m`

### Test 7: Diff View — **PASS** ✅
From prior session: tapping "package.json, Modified" opened a side-by-side diff tab titled "package.json (Working Tree), package.json" with line numbers 1-14 (left) and 1-17 (right). Code path: `GitService.swift` L64-74 handles `git.diff` → `NativeGitWriter.swift` L50-56 runs `git diff`.

#L1  import Foundation
#L2  
#L3  /// NativeGitWriter provides local git operations (add, commit, etc.)
#L4  /// using libgit2 or command-line git, bypassing the need for SSH connections.
#L5  class NativeGitWriter {
#L6      
#L7      private let repoPath: String
#L8      
#L9      init(repoPath: String) {
#L10         self.repoPath = repoPath
#L11     }
#L12     
#L13     // MARK: - Stage (git add)
#L14     
#L15     /// Stage a file for commit
#L16     func stage(file: String) throws {
#L17         let result = try runGit(["add", file])
#L18         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L19             throw GitError.stageFailed(result.stderr)
#L20         }
#L21     }
#L22     
#L23     /// Stage all changes
#L24     func stageAll() throws {
#L25         let result = try runGit(["add", "-A"])
#L26         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L27             throw GitError.stageFailed(result.stderr)
#L28         }
#L29     }
#L30     
#L31     // MARK: - Commit
#L32     
#L33     /// Create a local commit with the given message
#L34     func commit(message: String) throws {
#L35         // Stage all changes first if nothing is explicitly staged
#L36         let status = try runGit(["diff", "--cached", "--name-only"])
#L37         if status.stdout.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines).isEmpty {
#L38             try stageAll()
#L39         }
#L40         
#L41         let result = try runGit(["commit", "-m", message])
#L42         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L43             throw GitError.commitFailed(result.stderr)
#L44         }
#L45     }
#L46     
#L47     // MARK: - Diff
#L48     
#L49     /// Get diff for a specific file
#L50     func diff(file: String) throws -> String {
#L51         let result = try runGit(["diff", file])
#L52         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L53             throw GitError.diffFailed(result.stderr)
#L54         }
#L55         return result.stdout
#L56     }
#L57     
#L58     // MARK: - Status
#L59     
#L60     /// Get repository status
#L61     func status() throws -> String {
#L62         let result = try runGit(["status", "--porcelain"])
#L63         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L64             throw GitError.statusFailed(result.stderr)
#L65         }
#L66         return result.stdout
#L67     }
#L68     
#L69     // MARK: - Private Helpers
#L70     
#L71     private struct ProcessResult {
#L72         let stdout: String
#L73         let stderr: String
#L74         let exitCode: Int32
#L75     }
#L76     
#L77     private func runGit(_ arguments: [String]) throws -> ProcessResult {
#L78         let process = Process()
#L79         process.executableURL = URL(fileURLWithPath: "/usr/bin/git")
#L80         process.arguments = arguments
#L81         process.currentDirectoryURL = URL(fileURLWithPath: repoPath)
#L82         
#L83         let stdoutPipe = Pipe()
#L84         let stderrPipe = Pipe()
#L85         process.standardOutput = stdoutPipe
#L86         process.standardError = stderrPipe
#L87         
#L88         try process.run()
#L89         process.waitUntilExit()
#L90         
#L91         let stdoutData = stdoutPipe.fileHandleForReading.readDataToEndOfFile()
#L92         let stderrData = stderrPipe.fileHandleForReading.readDataToEndOfFile()
#L93         
#L94         return ProcessResult(
#L95             stdout: String(data: stdoutData, encoding: .utf8) ?? "",
#L96             stderr: String(data: stderrData, encoding: .utf8) ?? "",
#L97             exitCode: process.terminationStatus
#L98         )
#L99     }
#L100 }
#L101 
#L102 // MARK: - Errors
#L103 
#L104 enum GitError: LocalizedError {
#L105     case stageFailed(String)
#L106     case commitFailed(String)
#L107     case diffFailed(String)
#L108     case statusFailed(String)
#L109     
#L110     var errorDescription: String? {
#L111         switch self {
#L112         case .stageFailed(let msg): return "Stage failed: \(msg)"
#L113         case .commitFailed(let msg): return "Commit failed: \(msg)"
#L114         case .diffFailed(let msg): return "Diff failed: \(msg)"
#L115         case .statusFailed(let msg): return "Status failed: \(msg)"
#L116         }
#L117     }
#L118 }

#L1  import Foundation
#L2  import Combine
#L3  
#L4  /// GitService bridges the WebView's git commands to native implementations
#L5  class GitService: ObservableObject {
#L6      
#L7      @Published var isReady = false
#L8      
#L9      private var writer: NativeGitWriter?
#L10     private var repoPath: String?
#L11     
#L12     static let shared = GitService()
#L13     
#L14     // MARK: - Setup
#L15     
#L16     func configure(repoPath: String) {
#L17         self.repoPath = repoPath
#L18         self.writer = NativeGitWriter(repoPath: repoPath)
#L19         self.isReady = true
#L20     }
#L21     
#L22     // MARK: - WebView Message Handlers
#L23     
#L24     /// Handle git commands from the WebView JavaScript bridge
#L25     func handleCommand(_ command: String, params: [String: Any], completion: @escaping (Result<Any, Error>) -> Void) {
#L26         guard let writer = writer else {
#L27             completion(.failure(GitServiceError.notConfigured))
#L28             return
#L29         }
#L30         
#L31         switch command {
#L32         case "git.stage":
#L33             guard let file = params["file"] as? String else {
#L34                 completion(.failure(GitServiceError.missingParameter("file")))
#L35                 return
#L36             }
#L37             do {
#L38                 try writer.stage(file: file)
#L39                 completion(.success(true))
#L40             } catch {
#L41                 completion(.failure(error))
#L42             }
#L43             
#L44         case "git.stageAll":
#L45             do {
#L46                 try writer.stageAll()
#L47                 completion(.success(true))
#L48             } catch {
#L49                 completion(.failure(error))
#L50             }
#L51             
#L52         case "git.commit":
#L53             guard let message = params["message"] as? String else {
#L54                 completion(.failure(GitServiceError.missingParameter("message")))
#L55                 return
#L56             }
#L57             do {
#L58                 try writer.commit(message: message)
#L59                 completion(.success(true))
#L60             } catch {
#L61                 completion(.failure(error))
#L62             }
#L63             
#L64         case "git.diff":
#L65             guard let file = params["file"] as? String else {
#L66                 completion(.failure(GitServiceError.missingParameter("file")))
#L67                 return
#L68             }
#L69             do {
#L70                 let diff = try writer.diff(file: file)
#L71                 completion(.success(diff))
#L72             } catch {
#L73                 completion(.failure(error))
#L74             }
#L75             
#L76         case "git.status":
#L77             do {
#L78                 let status = try writer.status()
#L79                 completion(.success(status))
#L80             } catch {
#L81                 completion(.failure(error))
#L82             }
#L83             
#L84         default:
#L85             completion(.failure(GitServiceError.unknownCommand(command)))
#L86         }
#L87     }
#L88 }
#L89 
#L90 // MARK: - Errors
#L91 
#L92 enum GitServiceError: LocalizedError {
#L93     case notConfigured
#L94     case missingParameter(String)
#L95     case unknownCommand(String)
#L96     
#L97     var errorDescription: String? {
#L98         switch self {
#L99         case .notConfigured: return "Git service not configured - no repository path set"
#L100        case .missingParameter(let p): return "Missing parameter: \(p)"
#L101        case .unknownCommand(let c): return "Unknown git command: \(c)"
#L102    }
#L103    }
#L104 }

#L1  /**
#L2   * Native Host - detects and interfaces with the iOS native shell
#L3   */
#L4  
#L5  export function isRunningInNativeHost(): boolean {
#L6    return !!window.webkit?.messageHandlers?.gitBridge;
#L7  }
#L8  
#L9  export function getNativeCapabilities() {
#L10   return {
#L11     git: isRunningInNativeHost(),
#L12     localFs: true,
#L13     ssh: false, // SSH no longer needed - using native git
#L14   };
#L15 }

#L1  /**
#L2   * Git Bridge - connects VSCode's git extension to native Swift git operations
#L3   * via WKWebView message handlers.
#L4   */
#L5  
#L6  interface NativeCallbackResult {
#L7    success: boolean;
#L8    data?: string;
#L9    error?: string;
#L10 }
#L11 
#L12 type CallbackFn = (result: NativeCallbackResult) => void;
#L13 
#L14 // Global callback registry
#L15 declare global {
#L16   interface Window {
#L17     _nativeCallbacks: Record<string, CallbackFn>;
#L18     webkit?: {
#L19       messageHandlers?: {
#L20         gitBridge?: {
#L21           postMessage(body: unknown): void;
#L22         };
#L23       };
#L24     };
#L25   }
#L26 }
#L27 
#L28 window._nativeCallbacks = window._nativeCallbacks || {};
#L29 
#L30 let callbackCounter = 0;
#L31 
#L32 function callNative(command: string, params: Record<string, unknown> = {}): Promise<string> {
#L33   return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
#L34     const callbackId = `cb_${++callbackCounter}_${Date.now()}`;
#L35     
#L36     window._nativeCallbacks[callbackId] = (result: NativeCallbackResult) => {
#L37       delete window._nativeCallbacks[callbackId];
#L38       if (result.success) {
#L39         resolve(result.data || '');
#L40       } else {
#L41         reject(new Error(result.error || 'Unknown native error'));
#L42       }
#L43     };
#L44     
#L45     if (window.webkit?.messageHandlers?.gitBridge) {
#L46       window.webkit.messageHandlers.gitBridge.postMessage({
#L47         command,
#L48         params,
#L49         callbackId
#L50       });
#L51     } else {
#L52       delete window._nativeCallbacks[callbackId];
#L53       reject(new Error('Native git bridge not available'));
#L54     }
#L55   });
#L56 }
#L57 
#L58 // Public API
#L59 export async function gitStage(file: string): Promise<void> {
#L60   await callNative('git.stage', { file });
#L61 }
#L62 
#L63 export async function gitStageAll(): Promise<void> {
#L64   await callNative('git.stageAll');
#L65 }
#L66 
#L67 export async function gitCommit(message: string): Promise<void> {
#L68   await callNative('git.commit', { message });
#L69 }
#L70 
#L71 export async function gitDiff(file: string): Promise<string> {
#L72   return callNative('git.diff', { file });
#L73 }
#L74 
#L75 export async function gitStatus(): Promise<string> {
#L76   return callNative('git.status');
#L77 }

#L1  import Foundation
#L2  import WebKit
#L3  
#L4  /// Coordinates messages between the WKWebView and native Swift services
#L5  class WebViewCoordinator: NSObject, WKScriptMessageHandler {
#L6      
#L7      private let gitService = GitService.shared
#L8      
#L9      func userContentController(_ userContentController: WKUserContentController,
#L10                                 didReceive message: WKScriptMessage) {
#L11         guard let body = message.body as? [String: Any],
#L12               let command = body["command"] as? String else {
#L13             return
#L14         }
#L15         
#L16         let params = body["params"] as? [String: Any] ?? [:]
#L17         let callbackId = body["callbackId"] as? String
#L18         
#L19         switch message.name {
#L20         case "gitBridge":
#L21             gitService.handleCommand(command, params: params) { [weak self] result in
#L22                 guard let callbackId = callbackId else { return }
#L23                 DispatchQueue.main.async {
#L24                     self?.sendCallback(callbackId: callbackId, result: result, to: message.webView)
#L25                 }
#L26             }
#L27         default:
#L28             break
#L29         }
#L30     }
#L31     
#L32     private func sendCallback(callbackId: String, result: Result<Any, Error>, to webView: WKWebView?) {
#L33         let js: String
#L34         switch result {
#L35         case .success(let value):
#L36             let encoded = (value as? String)?.replacingOccurrences(of: "'", with: "\\'") ?? "\(value)"
#L37             js = "window._nativeCallbacks['\(callbackId)']({success: true, data: '\(encoded)'})"
#L38         case .failure(let error):
#L39             let msg = error.localizedDescription.replacingOccurrences(of: "'", with: "\\'")
#L40             js = "window._nativeCallbacks['\(callbackId)']({success: false, error: '\(msg)'})"
#L41         }
#L42         webView?.evaluateJavaScript(js, completionHandler: nil)
#L43     }
#L44 }

#L1  import Foundation
#L2  
#L3  /// NativeGitWriter provides local git operations (add, commit, etc.)
#L4  /// using libgit2 or command-line git, bypassing the need for SSH connections.
#L5  class NativeGitWriter {
#L6      
#L7      private let repoPath: String
#L8      
#L9      init(repoPath: String) {
#L10         self.repoPath = repoPath
#L11     }
#L12     
#L13     // MARK: - Stage (git add)
#L14     
#L15     /// Stage a file for commit
#L16     func stage(file: String) throws {
#L17         let result = try runGit(["add", file])
#L18         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L19             throw GitError.stageFailed(result.stderr)
#L20         }
#L21     }
#L22     
#L23     /// Stage all changes
#L24     func stageAll() throws {
#L25         let result = try runGit(["add", "-A"])
#L26         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L27             throw GitError.stageFailed(result.stderr)
#L28         }
#L29     }
#L30     
#L31     // MARK: - Commit
#L32     
#L33     /// Create a local commit with the given message
#L34     func commit(message: String) throws {
#L35         // Stage all changes first if nothing is explicitly staged
#L36         let status = try runGit(["diff", "--cached", "--name-only"])
#L37         if status.stdout.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines).isEmpty {
#L38             try stageAll()
#L39         }
#L40         
#L41         let result = try runGit(["commit", "-m", message])
#L42         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L43             throw GitError.commitFailed(result.stderr)
#L44         }
#L45     }
#L46     
#L47     // MARK: - Diff
#L48     
#L49     /// Get diff for a specific file
#L50     func diff(file: String) throws -> String {
#L51         let result = try runGit(["diff", file])
#L52         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L53             throw GitError.diffFailed(result.stderr)
#L54         }
#L55         return result.stdout
#L56     }
#L57     
#L58     // MARK: - Status
#L59     
#L60     /// Get repository status
#L61     func status() throws -> String {
#L62         let result = try runGit(["status", "--porcelain"])
#L63         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L64             throw GitError.statusFailed(result.stderr)
#L65         }
#L66         return result.stdout
#L67     }
#L68     
#L69     // MARK: - Private Helpers
#L70     
#L71     private struct ProcessResult {
#L72         let stdout: String
#L73         let stderr: String
#L74         let exitCode: Int32
#L75     }
#L76     
#L77     private func runGit(_ arguments: [String]) throws -> ProcessResult {
#L78         let process = Process()
#L79         process.executableURL = URL(fileURLWithPath: "/usr/bin/git")
#L80         process.arguments = arguments
#L81         process.currentDirectoryURL = URL(fileURLWithPath: repoPath)
#L82         
#L83         let stdoutPipe = Pipe()
#L84         let stderrPipe = Pipe()
#L85         process.standardOutput = stdoutPipe
#L86         process.standardError = stderrPipe
#L87         
#L88         try process.run()
#L89         process.waitUntilExit()
#L90         
#L91         let stdoutData = stdoutPipe.fileHandleForReading.readDataToEndOfFile()
#L92         let stderrData = stderrPipe.fileHandleForReading.readDataToEndOfFile()
#L93         
#L94         return ProcessResult(
#L95             stdout: String(data: stdoutData, encoding: .utf8) ?? "",
#L96             stderr: String(data: stderrData, encoding: .utf8) ?? "",
#L97             exitCode: process.terminationStatus
#L98         )
#L99     }
#L100 }
#L101 
#L102 // MARK: - Errors
#L103 
#L104 enum GitError: LocalizedError {
#L105     case stageFailed(String)
#L106     case commitFailed(String)
#L107     case diffFailed(String)
#L108     case statusFailed(String)
#L109     
#L110     var errorDescription: String? {
#L111         switch self {
#L112         case .stageFailed(let msg): return "Stage failed: \(msg)"
#L113         case .commitFailed(let msg): return "Commit failed: \(msg)"
#L114         case .diffFailed(let msg): return "Diff failed: \(msg)"
#L115         case .statusFailed(let msg): return "Status failed: \(msg)"
#L116         }
#L117     }
#L118 }

#L1  import Foundation
#L2  import Combine
#L3  
#L4  /// GitService bridges the WebView's git commands to native implementations
#L5  class GitService: ObservableObject {
#L6      
#L7      @Published var isReady = false
#L8      
#L9      private var writer: NativeGitWriter?
#L10     private var repoPath: String?
#L11     
#L12     static let shared = GitService()
#L13     
#L14     // MARK: - Setup
#L15     
#L16     func configure(repoPath: String) {
#L17         self.repoPath = repoPath
#L18         self.writer = NativeGitWriter(repoPath: repoPath)
#L19         self.isReady = true
#L20     }
#L21     
#L22     // MARK: - WebView Message Handlers
#L23     
#L24     /// Handle git commands from the WebView JavaScript bridge
#L25     func handleCommand(_ command: String, params: [String: Any], completion: @escaping (Result<Any, Error>) -> Void) {
#L26         guard let writer = writer else {
#L27             completion(.failure(GitServiceError.notConfigured))
#L28             return
#L29         }
#L30         
#L31         switch command {
#L32         case "git.stage":
#L33             guard let file = params["file"] as? String else {
#L34                 completion(.failure(GitServiceError.missingParameter("file")))
#L35                 return
#L36             }
#L37             do {
#L38                 try writer.stage(file: file)
#L39                 completion(.success(true))
#L40             } catch {
#L41                 completion(.failure(error))
#L42             }
#L43             
#L44         case "git.stageAll":
#L45             do {
#L46                 try writer.stageAll()
#L47                 completion(.success(true))
#L48             } catch {
#L49                 completion(.failure(error))
#L50             }
#L51             
#L52         case "git.commit":
#L53             guard let message = params["message"] as? String else {
#L54                 completion(.failure(GitServiceError.missingParameter("message")))
#L55                 return
#L56             }
#L57             do {
#L58                 try writer.commit(message: message)
#L59                 completion(.success(true))
#L60             } catch {
#L61                 completion(.failure(error))
#L62             }
#L63             
#L64         case "git.diff":
#L65             guard let file = params["file"] as? String else {
#L66                 completion(.failure(GitServiceError.missingParameter("file")))
#L67                 return
#L68             }
#L69             do {
#L70                 let diff = try writer.diff(file: file)
#L71                 completion(.success(diff))
#L72             } catch {
#L73                 completion(.failure(error))
#L74             }
#L75             
#L76         case "git.status":
#L77             do {
#L78                 let status = try writer.status()
#L79                 completion(.success(status))
#L80             } catch {
#L81                 completion(.failure(error))
#L82             }
#L83             
#L84         default:
#L85             completion(.failure(GitServiceError.unknownCommand(command)))
#L86         }
#L87     }
#L88 }
#L89 
#L90 // MARK: - Errors
#L91 
#L92 enum GitServiceError: LocalizedError {
#L93     case notConfigured

#L1  import Foundation
#L2  
#L3  /// NativeGitWriter provides local git operations (add, commit, etc.)
#L4  /// using libgit2 or command-line git, bypassing the need for SSH connections.
#L5  class NativeGitWriter {
#L6      
#L7      private let repoPath: String
#L8      
#L9      init(repoPath: String) {
#L10         self.repoPath = repoPath
#L11     }
#L12     
#L13     // MARK: - Stage (git add)
#L14     
#L15     /// Stage a file for commit
#L16     func stage(file: String) throws {
#L17         let result = try runGit(["add", file])
#L18         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L19             throw GitError.stageFailed(result.stderr)
#L20         }
#L21     }
#L22     
#L23     /// Stage all changes
#L24     func stageAll() throws {
#L25         let result = try runGit(["add", "-A"])
#L26         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L27             throw GitError.stageFailed(result.stderr)
#L28         }
#L29     }
#L30     
#L31     // MARK: - Commit
#L32     
#L33     /// Create a local commit with the given message
#L34     func commit(message: String) throws {
#L35         // Stage all changes first if nothing is explicitly staged
#L36         let status = try runGit(["diff", "--cached", "--name-only"])
#L37         if status.stdout.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines).isEmpty {
#L38             try stageAll()
#L39         }
#L40         
#L41         let result = try runGit(["commit", "-m", message])
#L42         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L43             throw GitError.commitFailed(result.stderr)
#L44         }
#L45     }
#L46     
#L47     // MARK: - Diff
#L48     
#L49     /// Get diff for a specific file
#L50     func diff(file: String) throws -> String {
#L51         let result = try runGit(["diff", file])
#L52         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L53             throw GitError.diffFailed(result.stderr)
#L54         }
#L55         return result.stdout
#L56     }
#L57     
#L58     // MARK: - Status
#L59     
#L60     /// Get repository status
#L61     func status() throws -> String {
#L62         let result = try runGit(["status", "--porcelain"])
#L63         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L64             throw GitError.statusFailed(result.stderr)
#L65         }
#L66         return result.stdout
#L67     }
#L68     
#L69     // MARK: - Private Helpers
#L70     
#L71     private struct ProcessResult {
#L72         let stdout: String
#L73         let stderr: String
#L74         let exitCode: Int32
#L75     }
#L76     
#L77     private func runGit(_ arguments: [String]) throws -> ProcessResult {
#L78         let process = Process()
#L79         process.executableURL = URL(fileURLWithPath: "/usr/bin/git")
#L80         process.arguments = arguments
#L81         process.currentDirectoryURL = URL(fileURLWithPath: repoPath)
#L82         
#L83         let stdoutPipe = Pipe()
#L84         let stderrPipe = Pipe()
#L85         process.standardOutput = stdoutPipe
#L86         process.standardError = stderrPipe
#L87         
#L88         try process.run()
#L89         process.waitUntilExit()
#L90         
#L91         let stdoutData = stdoutPipe.fileHandleForReading.readDataToEndOfFile()
#L92         let stderrData = stderrPipe.fileHandleForReading.readDataToEndOfFile()
#L93         
#L94         return ProcessResult(
#L95             stdout: String(data: stdoutData, encoding: .utf8) ?? "",
#L96             stderr: String(data: stderrData, encoding: .utf8) ?? "",
#L97             exitCode: process.terminationStatus
#L98         )
#L99     }
#L100 }
#L101 
#L102 // MARK: - Errors
#L103 
#L104 enum GitError: LocalizedError {
#L105     case stageFailed(String)
#L106     case commitFailed(String)
#L107     case diffFailed(String)
#L108     case statusFailed(String)
#L109     
#L110     var errorDescription: String? {
#L111         switch self {
#L112         case .stageFailed(let msg): return "Stage failed: \(msg)"
#L113         case .commitFailed(let msg): return "Commit failed: \(msg)"
#L114         case .diffFailed(let msg): return "Diff failed: \(msg)"
#L115         case .statusFailed(let msg): return "Status failed: \(msg)"
#L116         }
#L117     }
#L118 }

#L1  import Foundation
#L2  import Combine
#L3  
#L4  /// GitService bridges the WebView's git commands to native implementations
#L5  class GitService: ObservableObject {
#L6      
#L7      @Published var isReady = false
#L8      
#L9      private var writer: NativeGitWriter?
#L10     private var repoPath: String?
#L11     
#L12     static let shared = GitService()
#L13     
#L14     // MARK: - Setup
#L15     
#L16     func configure(repoPath: String) {
#L17         self.repoPath = repoPath
#L18         self.writer = NativeGitWriter(repoPath: repoPath)
#L19         self.isReady = true
#L20     }
#L21     
#L22     // MARK: - WebView Message Handlers
#L23     
#L24     /// Handle git commands from the WebView JavaScript bridge
#L25     func handleCommand(_ command: String, params: [String: Any], completion: @escaping (Result<Any, Error>) -> Void) {
#L26         guard let writer = writer else {
#L27             completion(.failure(GitServiceError.notConfigured))
#L28             return
#L29         }
#L30         
#L31         switch command {
#L32         case "git.stage":
#L33             guard let file = params["file"] as? String else {
#L34                 completion(.failure(GitServiceError.missingParameter("file")))
#L35                 return
#L36             }
#L37             do {
#L38                 try writer.stage(file: file)
#L39                 completion(.success(true))
#L40             } catch {
#L41                 completion(.failure(error))
#L42             }
#L43             
#L44         case "git.stageAll":
#L45             do {
#L46                 try writer.stageAll()
#L47                 completion(.success(true))
#L48             } catch {
#L49                 completion(.failure(error))
#L50             }
#L51             
#L52         case "git.commit":
#L53             guard let message = params["message"] as? String else {
#L54                 completion(.failure(GitServiceError.missingParameter("message")))
#L55                 return
#L56             }
#L57             do {
#L58                 try writer.commit(message: message)
#L59                 completion(.success(true))
#L60             } catch {
#L61                 completion(.failure(error))
#L62             }
#L63             
#L64         case "git.diff":
#L65             guard let file = params["file"] as? String else {
#L66                 completion(.failure(GitServiceError.missingParameter("file")))
#L67                 return
#L68             }
#L69             do {
#L70                 let diff = try writer.diff(file: file)
#L71                 completion(.success(diff))
#L72             } catch {
#L73                 completion(.failure(error))
#L74             }
#L75             
#L76         case "git.status":
#L77             do {
#L78                 let status = try writer.status()
#L79                 completion(.success(status))
#L80             } catch {
#L81                 completion(.failure(error))
#L82             }
#L83             
#L84         default:
#L85             completion(.failure(GitServiceError.unknownCommand(command)))
#L86         }
#L87     }
#L88 }
#L89 
#L90 // MARK: - Errors
#L91 
#L92 enum GitServiceError: LocalizedError {
#L93     case notConfigured
#L94     case missingParameter(String)
#L95     case unknownCommand(String)
#L96     
#L97     var errorDescription: String? {
#L98         switch self {
#L99         case .notConfigured: return "Git service not configured - no repository path set"
#L100        case .missingParameter(let p): return "Missing parameter: \(p)"
#L101        case .unknownCommand(let c): return "Unknown git command: \(c)"
#L102    }
#L103    }
#L104 }

#L1  import Foundation
#L2  
#L3  /// NativeGitWriter provides local git operations (add, commit, etc.)
#L4  /// using libgit2 or command-line git, bypassing the need for SSH connections.
#L5  class NativeGitWriter {
#L6      
#L7      private let repoPath: String
#L8      
#L9      init(repoPath: String) {
#L10         self.repoPath = repoPath
#L11     }
#L12     
#L13     // MARK: - Stage (git add)
#L14     
#L15     /// Stage a file for commit
#L16     func stage(file: String) throws {
#L17         let result = try runGit(["add", file])
#L18         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L19             throw GitError.stageFailed(result.stderr)
#L20         }
#L21     }
#L22     
#L23     /// Stage all changes
#L24     func stageAll() throws {
#L25         let result = try runGit(["add", "-A"])
#L26         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L27             throw GitError.stageFailed(result.stderr)
#L28         }
#L29     }
#L30     
#L31     // MARK: - Commit
#L32     
#L33     /// Create a local commit with the given message
#L34     func commit(message: String) throws {
#L35         // Stage all changes first if nothing is explicitly staged
#L36         let status = try runGit(["diff", "--cached", "--name-only"])
#L37         if status.stdout.trimmingCharacters(in: .whitespacesAndNewlines).isEmpty {
#L38             try stageAll()
#L39         }
#L40         
#L41         let result = try runGit(["commit", "-m", message])
#L42         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L43             throw GitError.commitFailed(result.stderr)
#L44         }
#L45     }
#L46     
#L47     // MARK: - Diff
#L48     
#L49     /// Get diff for a specific file
#L50     func diff(file: String) throws -> String {
#L51         let result = try runGit(["diff", file])
#L52         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L53             throw GitError.diffFailed(result.stderr)
#L54         }
#L55         return result.stdout
#L56     }
#L57     
#L58     // MARK: - Status
#L59     
#L60     /// Get repository status
#L61     func status() throws -> String {
#L62         let result = try runGit(["status", "--porcelain"])
#L63         guard result.exitCode == 0 else {
#L64             throw GitError.statusFailed(result.stderr)
#L65         }
#L66         return result.stdout
#L67     }
#L68     
#L69     // MARK: - Private Helpers
#L70     
#L71     private struct ProcessResult {
#L72         let stdout: String
#L73         let stderr: String
#L74         let exitCode: Int32
#L75     }
#L76     
#L77     private func runGit(_ arguments: [String]) throws -> ProcessResult {
#L78         let process = Process()
#L79         process.executableURL = URL(fileURLWithPath: "/usr/bin/git")
#L80         process.arguments = arguments
#L81         process.currentDirectoryURL = URL(fileURLWithPath: repoPath)
#L82         
#L83         let stdoutPipe = Pipe()
#L84         let stderrPipe = Pipe()
#L85         process.standardOutput = stdoutPipe
#L86         process.standardError = stderrPipe
#L87         
#L88         try process.run()
#L89         process.waitUntilExit()
#L90         
#L91         let stdoutData = stdoutPipe.fileHandleForReading.readDataToEndOfFile()
#L92         let stderrData = stderrPipe.fileHandleForReading.readDataToEndOfFile()
#L93         
#L94         return ProcessResult(
#L95             stdout: String(data: stdoutData, encoding: .utf8) ?? "",
#L96             stderr: String(data: stderrData, encoding: .utf8) ?? "",
#L97             exitCode: process.terminationStatus
#L98         )
#L99     }
#L100 }
#L101 
#L102 // MARK: - Errors
#L103 
#L104 enum GitError: LocalizedError {
#L105     case stageFailed(String)
#L106     case commitFailed(String)
#L107     case diffFailed(String)
#L108     case statusFailed(String)
#L109     
#L110     var errorDescription: String? {
#L111         switch self {
#L112         case .stageFailed(let msg): return "Stage failed: \(msg)"
#L113         case .commitFailed(let msg): return "Commit failed: \(msg)"
#L114         case .diffFailed(let msg): return "Diff failed: \(msg)"
#L115         case .statusFailed(let msg): return "Status failed: \(msg)"
#L116         }
#L117     }
#L118 }

#L1  import Foundation
#L2  import Combine
#L3  
#L4  /// GitService bridges the WebView's git commands to native implementations
#L5  class GitService: ObservableObject {
#L6      
#L7      @Published var isReady = false
#L8      
#L9      private var writer: NativeGitWriter?
#L10     private var repoPath: String?
#L11     
#L12     static let shared = GitService()
#L13     
#L14     // MARK: - Setup
#L15     
#L16     func configure(repoPath: String) {
#L17         self.repoPath = repoPath
#L18         self.writer = NativeGitWriter(repoPath: repoPath)
#L19         self.isReady = true
#L20     }
#L21     
#L22     // MARK: - WebView Message Handlers
#L23     
#L24     /// Handle git commands from the WebView JavaScript bridge
#L25     func handleCommand(_ command: String, params: [String: Any], completion: @escaping (Result<Any, Error>) -> Void) {
#L26         guard let writer = writer else {
#L27             completion(.failure(GitServiceError.notConfigured))
#L28             return
#L29         }
#L30         
#L31         switch command {
#L32         case "git.stage":
#L33             guard let file = params["file"] as? String else {
#L34                 completion(.failure(GitServiceError.missingParameter("file")))
#L35                 return
#L36             }
#L37             do {
#L38                 try writer.stage(file: file)
#L39                 completion(.success(true))
#L40             } catch {
#L41                 completion(.failure(error))
#L42             }
#L43             
#L44         case "git.stageAll":
#L45             do {
#L46                 try writer.stageAll()
#L47                 completion(.success(true))
#L48             } catch {
#L49                 completion(.failure(error))
#L50             }
#L51             
#L52         case "git.commit":
#L53             guard let message = params["message"] as? String else {
#L54                 completion(.failure(GitServiceError.missingParameter("message")))
#L55                 return
#L56             }
#L57             do {
#L58                 try writer.commit(message: message)
#L59                 completion(.success(true))
#L60             } catch {
#L61                 completion(.failure(error))
#L62             }
#L63             
#L64         case "git.diff":
#L65             guard let file = params["file"] as? String else {
#L66                 completion(.failure(GitServiceError.missingParameter("file")))
#L67                 return
#L68             }
#L69             do {
#L70                 let diff = try writer.diff(file: file)
#L71                 completion(.success(diff))
#L72             } catch {
#L73                 completion(.failure(error))
#L74             }
#L75             
#L76         case "git.status":
#L77             do {
#L78                 let status = try writer.status()
#L79                 completion(.success(status))
#L80             } catch {
#L81                 completion(.failure(error))
#L82             }
#L83             
#L84         default:
#L85             completion(.failure(GitServiceError.unknownCommand(command)))
#L86         }
#L87     }
#L88 }
#L89 
#L90 // MARK: - Errors
#L91 
#L92 enum GitServiceError: LocalizedError {
#L93     case notConfigured
#L94     case missingParameter(String)
#L95     case unknownCommand(String)
#L96     
#L97     var errorDescription: String? {
#L98         switch self {
#L99         case .notConfigured: return "Git service not configured - no repository path set"
#L100        case .missingParameter(let p): return "Missing parameter: \(p)"
#L101        case .unknownCommand(let c): return "Unknown git command: \(c)"
#L102    }
#L103    }
#L104 }

#L20         contentController.add(coordinator, name: "gitBridge")
#L21

#L23         config.preferences.setValue(true, forKey: "allowFileAccessFromFileURLs")
#L24         
#L25         webView = WKWebView(frame: view.bounds, configuration: config)
#L26         webView.autoresizingMask = [.flexibleWidth, .flexibleHeight]
#L27         view.addSubview(webView)
#L28     }
#L29     
#L30     private func loadVSCode() {
#L31         // Configure git service with the workspace path
#L32         if let docsPath = FileManager.default.urls(for: .documentDirectory, in: .userDomainMask).first {
#L33             let workspacePath = docsPath.appendingPathComponent("workspace").path
#L34             GitService.shared.configure(repoPath: workspacePath)
#L35         }
#L36         
#L37         // Load the VSCode web bundle
#L38         if let indexURL = Bundle.main.url(forResource: "index", withExtension: "html", subdirectory: "build") {
#L39             webView.loadFileURL(indexURL, allowingReadAccessTo: indexURL.deletingLastPathComponent())
#L40         }
#L41     }

200|6c7e60|    private func writeTree(node: TreeNode) throws -> String {
201|5fb70c|        var entries: [TreeEntry] = []
202|adc83b|
203|4ec453|        // Children trees first (hashes computed recursively)
204|e440fe|        for (name, child) in node.children {
205|37e775|            let childSha = try writeTree(node: child)
206|1dc17e|            entries.append(TreeEntry(mode: "40000", name: name, sha: childSha, isTree: true))
207|5f3077|        }
208|adc83b|
209|e75b5d|        // Blobs
210|6f8e62|        for (name, blob) in node.blobs {
211|b9f46a|            entries.append(TreeEntry(mode: blob.mode, name: name, sha: blob.sha, isTree: false))
212|5f3077|        }
213|adc83b|
214|0e513d|        // Git sorts entries by name, but compares directories as name + '/'
215|53a80f|        entries.sort { a, b in
216|2b9d07|            let aKey = a.name + (a.isTree ? "/" : "")
217|bd8876|            let bKey = b.name + (b.isTree ? "/" : "")
218|df330a|            return Self.lexicographicLess(aKey.utf8, bKey.utf8)
219|5f3077|        }
220|adc83b|
221|72d469|        var data = Data()

223|85ff94|            data.append(contentsOf: "\(entry.mode) \(entry.name)\u{0}".utf8)
224|eb0662|            data.append(contentsOf: try Self.hexToBytes(entry.sha))
225|5f3077|        }

227|1274f5|        return try writeObject(type: .tree, content: data)
228|27e597|    }
229|adc83b|
230|a5c85f|    private static func lexicographicLess(_ a: String.UTF8View, _ b: String.UTF8View) -> Bool {
231|f94110|        var ita = a.makeIterator()
232|aa5d5c|        var itb = b.makeIterator()
233|722ae9|        while true {
234|d0134b|            let ca = ita.next()
235|a32c82|            let cb = itb.next()
236|77efa3|            switch (ca, cb) {
237|61b1fe|            case let (x?, y?):
238|905acb|                if x != y { return x < y }
239|bbe0af|            case (nil, nil):
240|473d08|                return false
241|74eab7|            case (nil, _?):
242|50bdea|                return true
243|f4d5d4|            case (_?, nil):
244|473d08|                return false
245|a7dc16|            }
246|5f3077|        }
247|27e597|    }

253|bca733|        let header = "\(type.rawValue) \(content.count)\u{0}"

274|d78bc9|    private static func sha1Hex(_ data: Data) -> String {
275|2f8f19|        var digest = [UInt8](repeating: 0, count: Int(CC_SHA1_DIGEST_LENGTH))
276|8bad8d|        data.withUnsafeBytes { ptr in

282|5ba044|    private static func compressZlib(_ data: Data) throws -> Data {
283|3d9c6d|        // Compression framework needs a destination buffer large enough.
284|eb928d|        // Start with a reasonable guess and grow if needed.
285|0e4706|        var destSize = max(data.count / 2, 1024)
286|4b34fa|        for _ in 0..<6 {
287|7ab7ba|            let destBuffer = UnsafeMutablePointer<UInt8>.allocate(capacity: destSize)
288|23e0db|            defer { destBuffer.deallocate() }
289|adc83b|
290|c35693|            let written: Int = data.withUnsafeBytes { sourcePtr in
291|8af049|                guard let base = sourcePtr.baseAddress else { return 0 }
292|53473b|                return compression_encode_buffer(
293|8c4161|                    destBuffer,
294|871512|                    destSize,
295|08b8a6|                    base.assumingMemoryBound(to: UInt8.self),
296|b87b1c|                    data.count,
297|f3e974|                    nil,
298|4dc23f|                    COMPRESSION_ZLIB
299|6f642e|                )
300|a7dc16|            }
301|adc83b|
302|420212|            if written > 0 {
303|2c941e|                return Data(bytes: destBuffer, count: written)
304|a7dc16|            }
305|adc83b|
306|3a8e96|            // Increase and retry
307|a2e26f|            destSize *= 2
308|5f3077|        }
309|adc83b|
310|e3f56e|        throw GitManagerError.invalidRepository
311|27e597|    }

450|983731|    private func blobSHAFromTree(components: [String], treeSHA: String, reader: NativeGitReader) -> String? {
451|76a335|        guard !components.isEmpty,
452|043602|              let treeObj = reader.readObject(sha: treeSHA),
453|78bd0e|              treeObj.type == .tree else {
454|1c8557|            return nil
455|5f3077|        }
456|d6ed84|        
457|8fc0fb|        let entries = parseTreeEntriesForWrite(data: treeObj.data)
458|3d0308|        let head = components[0]
459|d6ed84|        
460|703828|        if components.count == 1 {
461|4c8d7b|            // Looking for a blob
462|ab8b97|            return entries.first { $0.name == head && !$0.mode.hasPrefix("40") }?.sha
463|b31999|        } else {
464|0521dc|            // Looking for a subtree
465|2b7757|            guard let dir = entries.first(where: { $0.name == head && $0.mode.hasPrefix("40") }) else {
466|15034a|                return nil
467|a7dc16|            }
468|b241d5|            return blobSHAFromTree(components: Array(components.dropFirst()), treeSHA: dir.sha, reader: reader)
469|5f3077|        }
470|27e597|    }
471|b4687f|    
472|b2b9ca|    private func parseTreeEntriesForWrite(data: Data) -> [(mode: String, name: String, sha: String)] {
473|10efd1|        var entries: [(String, String, String)] = []
474|2cb527|        var offset = 0
475|d6ed84|        
476|126a3b|        while offset < data.count {
477|67fc5d|            guard let spaceIndex = data[offset...].firstIndex(of: 0x20) else { break }
478|a3cc9c|            let modeData = data[offset..<spaceIndex]
479|6d483e|            guard let mode = String(data: modeData, encoding: .ascii) else { break }
480|3070d1|            
481|d36b62|            let nameStart = spaceIndex + 1
482|306227|            guard let nullIndex = data[nameStart...].firstIndex(of: 0) else { break }
483|327bc9|            let nameData = data[nameStart..<nullIndex]
484|237c3c|            guard let name = String(data: nameData, encoding: .utf8) else { break }
485|3070d1|            
486|c5842b|            let shaStart = nullIndex + 1
487|be9d3b|            let shaEnd = shaStart + 20
488|eb4a79|            guard shaEnd <= data.count else { break }
489|0075b7|            let shaData = data[shaStart..<shaEnd]
490|bb46c1|            let sha = shaData.map { String(format: "%02x", $0) }.joined()
491|3070d1|            
492|3e2294|            entries.append((mode, name, sha))
493|372dcb|            offset = shaEnd
494|5f3077|        }
495|d6ed84|        
496|f9dee7|        return entries
497|27e597|    }

499|83aa7b|    // MARK: - Index Writing
